                                <div class="question_title"><p>Accept Privacy Policy</p>
</div>

                                <div class="answers" ng-init="initRequireds( 1 )">

                                                                            
                                                                                    <div aside-field class="">
                                                <div id="privacybox" class="privacybox ps-child" aside-privacy-box>
                                                    <p><strong><span lang="EN-US">Privacy Policy</span></strong></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">Please be informed that Automobili Lamborghini S.p.A. in its quality of data controller (“Lamborghini”) will process your personal data in for the purposes specified below in accordance and in compliance with the EU Regulation 679/2016 (General Data Protection Regulation, the “Regulation”).</span></p>

<p><strong><span lang="EN-US">Purposes and legal bases of processing.</span></strong></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">Lamborghini collects and processes the personal data you provide for the following purposes:</span></p>

<p><strong><em><span lang="EN-US">a)</span></em></strong><span lang="EN-US">As far as the questionnaire is concerned, data such as IP address, gender, country of origin and age are treated for <em>Analysis and Research purposes</em></span></p>

<p><strong><em><span lang="EN-US">b)</span></em></strong><span lang="EN-US"> With reference to the email address only, for <em>Marketing purposes</em> related to the completion of market research and recognition of customer satisfaction, as well as the dispatch of promotional material regarding products, services, initiatives and events Offered by Lamborghini.</span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">For the purposes of which to the point a) to confer the data is necessary and functional to the regular completion of survey. In the absence you cannot participate in the survey</span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">The provision of the data specified in letter b) is required in order to be contacted by Lamborghini for marketing purposes: otherwise, the completion of the service survey will not be affected, but it will not be possible to be involved in market research and/or satisfaction detection, as well as to receive promotional communications concerning products, services, initiatives and projects offered </span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">by Lamborghini.</span></p>

<p><strong><span lang="EN-US">Methods of processing and storage of personal data</span></strong></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">Lamborghini processes your personal data either with or without electronic tools, and in any case in compliance with security requirements requested by applicable laws. </span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">All the answers provided are processed equally in aggregated and anonymous forms. </span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">The address mail eventually provided by the consumer at the end of the survey for the purpose specified in letter b) won’t be connected in any way to the given answers. </span></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">Your personal data are kept for the time strictly necessary to the pursuit of the purposes for which they are collected and for the fulfilment of applicable law and regulation obligations. The data will be deleted or anonymized in order to reach the above mentioned purposes, unless Lamborghini is obliged to retain the data for a further period in order to fulfil the obligations of law or regulation.</span></p>

<p><strong><span lang="EN-US">Disclosure of your personal data to third parties</span></strong></p>

<p><span lang="EN-US">Your personal data will not be communicated to third parties or disseminated.</span></p>

<p><strong><span lang="EN-US">Controller and data protection officer </span></strong></p>

<p><span>Automobili Lamborghini S.p.A., with registered office in via Modena 12, 40019 Sant’Agata Bolognese (BO), Italy is the Data controller. </span><span lang="EN-US">The Data protection officer is domicilied in the Data controller’s offices and can be contacted at the following email address: <span><a href="mailto:dpo@lamborghini.com">dpo@lamborghini.com</a></span>.</span></p>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var scripts=['//s7.addthis.com/js/300/addthis_widget.js#pubid=ra-58130d6e7c1b0811'];

    var loadScripts=function(){
        var el = document.createElement("script");
        el.onload=function() {
            if(scripts.length>0)
            {
                loadScripts();
            }else{
                try{window.addthislistener();}catch(e){}
            }
        };
        el.src=scripts.shift();
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(el);
    }

    loadScripts();

</script>
